<p><b>Eden Michael Hazard</b> (<small>French pronunciation:&#160;&#8203;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/French" title="Help:IPA/French">[edn aza]</a></span>; born 7 January 1991) is a Belgian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Winger_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Winger (association football)">winger</a> or <a href="/wiki/Attacking_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Attacking midfielder">attacking midfielder</a> for Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captains</a> the <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium national team</a>. He is known for his creativity, <a href="/wiki/Dribbling" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> and <a href="/wiki/Passing_(association_football)" title="Passing (association football)">passing</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard is the son of two former footballers and began his career in Belgium playing for local youth clubs. In 2005, he moved to France, where he began his senior career with <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> club <a href="/wiki/Lille_OSC" title="Lille OSC">Lille</a>. Hazard spent two years in the club's academy and, at the age of 16, made his professional debut in November 2007. He became an integral part of the Lille team under manager <a href="/wiki/Rudi_Garcia" title="Rudi Garcia">Rudi Garcia</a>. In his first full season, he became the first non-French player to win the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Young_Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Ligue 1 Young Player of the Year</a> award,<sup id="cite_ref-Lille_OSC_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lille_OSC-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> and the following season became the first player to win the award twice.<sup id="cite_ref-young_player_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-young_player-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_in_French_football" title="201011 in French football">201011 season</a>, he was a part of the Lille team that won the <a href="/wiki/Double_(association_football)" title="Double (association football)">league and cup double</a> and, as a result of his performances, was named the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Ligue 1 Player of the Year</a>, the youngest player to win the award.<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_player_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_player-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After making over 190 appearances and scoring 50 goals for Lille, Hazard signed for English club <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in June 2012. He won the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> in his first season and the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Young_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Young Player of the Year">PFA Young Player of the Year</a> in his second. In the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_in_English_football" title="201415 in English football">201415 season</a>, Hazard helped Chelsea win the <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">League Cup</a> and <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a>, earning him the <a href="/wiki/FWA_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="FWA Footballer of the Year">FWA Footballer of the Year</a> and the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a> awards. Two years later he won his second English league title as Chelsea won the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Premier_League" title="201617 Premier League">201617</a> Premier League. In 2018, he won the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_FA_Cup" title="201718 FA Cup">FA Cup</a>, and was named in the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_FIFPro_World_XI" class="mw-redirect" title="FIFA FIFPro World XI">FIFA FIFPro World XI</a>. He won the Europa League again with Chelsea in June 2019, then joined Real Madrid in a transfer worth up to 150 million,<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> winning <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> during his injury-plagued debut season.
</p><p>Having represented his country at various <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_youth_football_team" title="Belgium national youth football team">youth levels</a>, Hazard made his senior debut for the <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium national team</a> in November 2008, aged 17, in a <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game#Association_football" title="Exhibition game">friendly match</a> against <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg_national_football_team" title="Luxembourg national football team">Luxembourg</a>. Nearly three years after his debut, Hazard scored his first international goal against <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan_national_football_team" title="Kazakhstan national football team">Kazakhstan</a> in October 2011. He has since earned over 100 caps, and was a member of the Belgian squad which reached the quarter-finals of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>. At the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>, he captained Belgium to third place which was their best finish in history, receiving the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Ball_(FIFA)" class="mw-redirect" title="Golden Ball (FIFA)">Silver Ball</a> as the second-best player of the tournament.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Hazard was born in <a href="/wiki/La_Louvi%C3%A8re" title="La Louvière">La Louvière</a> and grew up in <a href="/wiki/Braine-le-Comte" title="Braine-le-Comte">Braine-le-Comte</a>. His mother Carine, and father Thierry, were both footballers. His father spent most of his career at <a href="/wiki/Semi-professional" class="mw-redirect" title="Semi-professional">semi-professional</a> level with <a href="/wiki/R.A.A._Louvi%C3%A9roise" title="R.A.A. Louviéroise">La Louvière</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Belgian_Second_Division" title="Belgian Second Division">Belgian Second Division</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-eden_leparisien_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_leparisien-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> playing mainly as a <a href="/wiki/Defensive_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Defensive midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_leparisien_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_leparisien-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> His mother played as a <a href="/wiki/Striker_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Striker (association football)">striker</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Belgian_Women%27s_First_Division" title="Belgian Women&#39;s First Division">Belgian Women's First Division</a> and stopped playing when she was three months pregnant with Eden.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_leparisien_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_leparisien-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-eden_family_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_family-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> After playing football, both parents became sports teachers.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_leparisien_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_leparisien-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Thierry retired from his position in 2009 in order to devote more time to his children.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_leparisien_13-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_leparisien-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard is the eldest of four children. He has three brothers, all of whom play football, including <a href="/wiki/Thorgan_Hazard" title="Thorgan Hazard">Thorgan</a>, who joined him at <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in 2012 but then moved to <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a> in 2015 and further to <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> in 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Thorgan had previously progressed through the youth ranks of Lille's <a href="/wiki/Derby_du_Nord" title="Derby du Nord">biggest rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">Lens</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-eden_hazard_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_hazard-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Hazard's other younger brothers are <a href="/wiki/Kylian_Hazard" title="Kylian Hazard">Kylian</a> and Ethan. On 15 July 2013, Kylian joined <a href="/wiki/R._White_Star_Bruxelles" class="mw-redirect" title="R. White Star Bruxelles">White Star Bruxelles</a>, but then went on to play for Hungarian side <a href="/wiki/%C3%9Ajpest_FC" title="Újpest FC">Újpest</a>, before also joining Chelsea,<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> while Ethan remains playing in the youth academy of Eden's former club <a href="/wiki/A.F.C._Tubize" title="A.F.C. Tubize">Tubize</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_leparisien_13-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_leparisien-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-eden_hazard_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_hazard-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard and his three brothers were raised in a comfortable environment with their parents ensuring they had whatever they needed to excel.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_hazard2_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_hazard2-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> The family lived "no more than three metres" from a football training ground and the brothers often ventured onto a training pitch through a small hole in order to hone and develop their skills.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_family_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_family-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Growing up his idol was French playmaker <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>, with Hazard "watching him on television and online for hours."<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Hazard began his football career playing for hometown club Royal Stade Brainois at the age of four. During his time at the club, one of his youth coaches described him as a "gifted" player. He added: "He knew everything. I had nothing to teach him".<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Hazard spent eight years at the club before moving to <a href="/wiki/A.F.C._Tubize" title="A.F.C. Tubize">Tubize</a>. While at Tubize, he was spotted by a Lille scout while playing in a local tournament with the club. The scout's subsequent report on the player prompted club officials to meet with Hazard's father and offer the young player an <i>aspirant</i> (youth) contract.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_contract_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_contract-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard's parents accepted the offer from Lille with hopes that the training facilities in France would be better.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_hazard2_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_hazard2-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Hazard's father later admitted that the decision to let Eden and, later Thorgan, join clubs in the <a href="/wiki/Nord-Pas-de-Calais" title="Nord-Pas-de-Calais">North of France</a> was the best solution stating "They remained so close to home and, at the same time, they integrated at structures where they could grow, because in Belgium, unfortunately, it's a little empty for the training of youth".<sup id="cite_ref-eden_family_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_family-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lille">Lille</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Lille">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Hazard joined Lille in 2005 and spent two years developing in the club's local sports school, due to its youth academy in Luchin not being in operation at that time.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> On 28 May 2007, he signed his first professional contract agreeing to a three-year deal with Lille.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_contract_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_contract-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> At the start of the <a href="/wiki/2007-08_Ligue_1" class="mw-redirect" title="2007-08 Ligue 1">200708 season</a>, at the age of 16, Hazard was promoted to the club's reserve team in the <a href="/wiki/Championnat_de_France_amateur" class="mw-redirect" title="Championnat de France amateur">Championnat de France amateur</a>, the fourth level of <a href="/wiki/Football_in_France" title="Football in France">French football</a>, though he still played with Lille's under-18 team in its league and the <a href="/wiki/Coupe_Gambardella" title="Coupe Gambardella">Coupe Gambardella</a>. Hazard made his amateur debut on 1 September 2007 in a league match against <a href="/wiki/Racing_Levallois_92" class="mw-redirect" title="Racing Levallois 92">Racing Club de France</a> appearing as a second-half substitute in a 31 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> He made his first start a week later in the team's 10 defeat to <a href="/wiki/US_Lesquin" title="US Lesquin">Lesquin</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After spending the majority of October and the early part of November playing with the club's under-18 team, on 14 November, due to several players being on international duty, Hazard was called up to the senior team by manager <a href="/wiki/Claude_Puel" title="Claude Puel">Claude Puel</a> to participate in a friendly match against Belgian club <a href="/wiki/FC_Bruges" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Bruges">Bruges</a> on 16 November.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He appeared as a substitute in the match and, as a result of his performance, was included in the 18-man squad to face <a href="/wiki/AS_Nancy" title="AS Nancy">Nancy</a> in a league match on 24 November,<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> where he subsequently made his professional debut in the match, coming on as a substitute in the 78th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard returned to the club's reserve team and spent December playing with the squad. Following the winter break, Hazard returned to the first team in January and made substitute appearances in three league matches against <a href="/wiki/FC_Metz" title="FC Metz">Metz</a>, <a href="/wiki/FC_Sochaux-Montb%C3%A9liard" title="FC Sochaux-Montbéliard">Sochaux</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Following the match against PSG, he was demoted back to amateur level where he played concurrently with the reserve team in the fourth division and the under-18 team in the Coupe Gambardella. On 17 May 2008, he scored his first amateur goal in a 32 victory over <a href="/wiki/AS_Vitr%C3%A9" title="AS Vitré">Vitré</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Hazard finished his amateur career with 11 appearances and one goal, helping the reserve team finished in fifth place, which was first among professional clubs' reserve teams playing in the group.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2008.E2.80.9310:_Debut_season_and_individual_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="200810:_Debut_season_and_individual_success">200810: Debut season and individual success</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 200810: Debut season and individual success">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>For the <a href="/wiki/2008-09_Ligue_1" class="mw-redirect" title="2008-09 Ligue 1">200809</a> season, Hazard was given the number&#160;26 shirt after playing with the number&#160;33 shirt in his debut season. He was also promoted to the senior team permanently by new manager <a href="/wiki/Rudi_Garcia" title="Rudi Garcia">Rudi Garcia</a>. Early on, he made substitute appearances regularly, including against <a href="/wiki/AJ_Auxerre" title="AJ Auxerre">Auxerre</a> on 20 September, when he scored a goal to make it 22 in the 88th minute in a game Lille won 32 in <a href="/wiki/Injury_time" class="mw-redirect" title="Injury time">injury time</a> following a goal from <a href="/wiki/Tulio_de_Melo" class="mw-redirect" title="Tulio de Melo">Tulio de Melo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Hazard's first career goal resulted in him becoming the youngest goalscorer in the club's history.<sup id="cite_ref-Lille_OSC_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lille_OSC-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Four days after scoring his first goal, Hazard made his first senior start in a 42 defeat on <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Penalty shootout (association football)">penalties</a> to <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="Coupe de la Ligue">Coupe de la Ligue</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> After featuring as a substitute in the team's next five league matches, on 15 November, Hazard started his first league game against <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a>, and capped the appearance by scoring the opening goal in the club's 30 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> His assured performances with the club resulted in Lille offering him a three-year contract extension, which he agreed to on 18 November 2008, tying him to the club until 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>
After featuring as a substitute in December, Hazard returned to the starting lineup in January. In February, he scored the match-winning goal in a league match against <a href="/wiki/FC_Sochaux-Montb%C3%A9liard" title="FC Sochaux-Montbéliard">Sochaux</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> In the Round of 16 of the Coupe de France, Hazard netted a goal in a 32 win over the competition's <a href="/wiki/2008_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="2008 Coupe de France Final">defending champions</a> <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Lyon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> In the final ten league matches of the campaign, Hazard started eight and contributed to the team finishing in fifth place, which resulted in Lille qualifying for the newly created <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a>. After the season, he was named the National Union of Professional Footballers (UNFP) <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Young_Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Young Player of the Year</a>, becoming the first international player to achieve the honour.<sup id="cite_ref-young_player_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-young_player-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></p><div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:30%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">Eden is technically gifted and very fast. He will be a major star in the future. I would take him to <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> with my eyes closed.</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a> on the 19-year-old Eden Hazard, August 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Following the 200809 season, constant media speculation occurred in numerous countries regarding Hazard's availability on the transfer market. Despite Lille chairman Michel Seydoux declaring the player off limits and Hazard stating that he wanted to remain at the club for at least another season, several clubs declared interest in the player.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> These included English clubs <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>, Italian club <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a>, and Spanish clubs <a href="/wiki/F.C._Barcelona" class="mw-redirect" title="F.C. Barcelona">Barcelona</a> and <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a>. Frenchman <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a> personally recommended the player to the latter club.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard began the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_in_French_football" title="200910 in French football">200910 season</a> on a positive note scoring in Lille's first competitive match of the season. The goal, contributing to the team's 20 victory, came against Serbian club <a href="/wiki/FK_Sevojno" title="FK Sevojno">FK Sevojno</a> in the first leg of the club's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League_2009-10#Third_qualifying_round" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA Europa League 2009-10">third qualifying round</a> match in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> On 27 August, he scored his second career <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">European</a> goal in the club's second leg tie in the playoff round against Belgian club <a href="/wiki/KRC_Genk" class="mw-redirect" title="KRC Genk">Genk</a>. It was Lille's final goal in the club's 42 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> The 63 aggregate scoreline assured the club progression to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> group stage.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>On 22 October, Hazard scored a goal in Lille's important 30 victory over Italian club <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a> in the 84th minute after entering as a substitute 10 minutes prior. Upon receiving the ball on the left wing, Hazard proceeded to dash through the midfield dribbling past six Genoa defenders before finishing at the 18-yard box.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> A month later, Hazard was instrumental in Lille's 51 thrashing of Czech club <a href="/wiki/Slavia_Prague" class="mw-redirect" title="Slavia Prague">Slavia Prague</a> as he was partly responsible for the opening goal slicing through the defense and delivering a cross near post, which went off Slavia player <a href="/wiki/Marek_Such%C3%BD" title="Marek Suchý">Marek Suchý</a> resulting in an <a href="/wiki/Own_goal" title="Own goal">own goal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 20 December, Hazard scored his first league goal of the season in the club's 30 win over <a href="/wiki/Le_Mans_Union_Club_72" class="mw-redirect" title="Le Mans Union Club 72">Le Mans</a>, as well as assisting the other two.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> On 30 January, Hazard scored the only goal in Lille's win over Derby du Nord rivals <a href="/wiki/RC_Lens" title="RC Lens">Lens</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Five days later, Hazard and Lille reached an agreement on a contract extension, which will keep the player at the club until 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 11 March, Hazard scored the only goal in Lille's victory over English club <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> in the first leg of the club's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> tie converting a <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">free kick</a> in the 83rd minute.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Three weeks later, Hazard provided two assists in the club's 41 win over title rivals <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> For his impressive displays in the month of March, Hazard was given the <a href="/wiki/UNFP_Player_of_the_Month" title="UNFP Player of the Month">UNFP Player of the Month</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 29 April, Hazard was nominated for the UNFP <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Player of the Year</a> award. He was also nominated, for the second consecutive season, for the Young Player of the Year award.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> On 9 May, Hazard was awarded the UNFP Young Player of the Year trophy for the second consecutive season. He became the first player since its inception in 1994 to win the award twice.<sup id="cite_ref-young_player_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-young_player-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Hazard lost out on the Player of the Year award, which was awarded to Lyon <a href="/wiki/Striker_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Striker (association football)">striker</a> <a href="/wiki/Lisandro_L%C3%B3pez" title="Lisandro López">Lisandro López</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.9311:_League_double.2C_Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year_and_continued_individual_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201011:_League_double,_Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year_and_continued_individual_success">201011: League double, Ligue 1 Player of the Year and continued individual success</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 201011: League double, Ligue 1 Player of the Year and continued individual success">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Hazard began the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_in_French_football" title="201011 in French football">201011 campaign</a> as a starter featuring in Lille's first six league matches of the season, as well as matches in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a>. On 29 August, he scored his first goal of the season in a 11 draw with <a href="/wiki/OGC_Nice" title="OGC Nice">Nice</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> In late September, Hazard began to struggle with inconsistency and was benched by Garcia in an effort to "allow him to breathe and learn that his performances were insufficient".<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_fourfourtwo_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_fourfourtwo-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Hazard later admitted that his first bout of inconsistency affected him stating "The first two months were a bit tough. I wouldn't say that I began doubting my abilities, but I definitely went through a really patchy spell".<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_fifa_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_fifa-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 October, Belgium national team manager <a href="/wiki/Georges_Leekens" title="Georges Leekens">Georges Leekens</a>, citing Hazard's recent spell on the bench at Lille, said that the player needed to work harder, both physically and mentally, to regain his past year's form. The team's assistant coach, <a href="/wiki/Marc_Wilmots" title="Marc Wilmots">Marc Wilmots</a>, also stated that Hazard often displayed a lazy mentality while training with the national team.<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_leekens_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_leekens-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Garcia responded to Leekens comments the following day stating that he thought they were "excessive" and that "Eden is only 19 years old" and can still "make more progress in all areas."<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Following Belgium's match against <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan_national_football_team" title="Kazakhstan national football team">Kazakhstan</a>, in which Hazard failed to start or even appear on the substitute's bench, Leekens responded to Garcia's comments declaring that he would stand by his previous comments and that players must think about the team and not themselves.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Hazard, himself, later reflected on Leekens and Garcia comments in February 2011 stating "I learned a lot during those few weeks, mentally speaking. And since then things have got better. The national side has had a fair bit to do with that  I get a lot out of being a part of it".<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_fifa_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_fifa-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the international break, he scored his second league goal of the season in a 31 win against the league leaders <a href="/wiki/Stade_Brestois_29" title="Stade Brestois 29">Brest</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> On 21 November, Hazard assisted both Lille's goals in a 21 win over <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> The victory continued the club's domestic unbeaten streak, which led to Lille topping the league table following an emphatic 63 victory against <a href="/wiki/FC_Lorient" title="FC Lorient">Lorient</a> on 5 December.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> At the turn of the calendar year, Hazard scored in the team's first match against amateur club <a href="/wiki/US_Forbach" title="US Forbach">Forbach</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a>. Lille won the match 31.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> In the team's following match, he assisted goals scored by <a href="/wiki/Moussa_Sow" title="Moussa Sow">Moussa Sow</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gervinho" title="Gervinho">Gervinho</a> in a 20 league victory over <a href="/wiki/OGC_Nice" title="OGC Nice">Nice</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 January, Hazard scored the second goal in a 30 victory over <a href="/wiki/AS_Nancy" title="AS Nancy">Nancy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> On 4 March, Lille officials confirmed that Hazard had signed a new contract until 2015, a deal which also made him the highest paid player in Ligue 1.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> In his first match after the news, Hazard scored the opening goal in Lille's 21 away win over title rivals Marseille.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> The goal was scored on a left-footed shot from almost 35 metres (38&#160;yd) out and was clocked at 95&#160;km/h (59&#160;mph).<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> On 2 April, Hazard capped his 100th league appearance with Lille by scoring the second goal in a 31 win over Caen.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> The goal tied his career-high for goals in a season and also moved Lille eight points clear at the top of the league table.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> For his performances in the month of March, Hazard was named the UNFP Player of the Month for the second time in his career.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> On 19 April, after appearing as a first-half substitute, he scored the opening goal in Lille's 20 Coupe de France semi-final victory over <a href="/wiki/OGC_Nice" title="OGC Nice">Nice</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> The victory inserted the club into the <a href="/wiki/2011_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="2011 Coupe de France Final">2011 Coupe de France Final</a>; the club's first appearance in the competition's final since <a href="/wiki/1955_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="1955 Coupe de France Final">1955</a>. On 7 May, Hazard converted a game-winning free-kick goal in the team's 10 win over Nancy.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he was nominated for the Ligue 1 Player of the Year award for the second consecutive season.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2011_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="2011 Coupe de France Final">Coupe de France final</a>, Hazard played 89 minutes as Lille defeated PSG 10 at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> A week later, Lille clinched the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Ligue_1" title="201011 Ligue 1">Ligue 1 title</a> by drawing 22 away to PSG, achieving the club's first league championship since the <a href="/wiki/1953%E2%80%9354_French_Division_1" title="195354 French Division 1">195354 season</a> and the club's first <a href="/wiki/Double_(association_football)" title="Double (association football)">double</a> since the <a href="/wiki/1945%E2%80%9346_French_Division_1" title="194546 French Division 1">194546 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> The domestic cup and league title were the first two honours in Hazard's career. On the day after Lille won the league, Hazard was named the Ligue 1 Player of the Year becoming the youngest player ever to win the award.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> He was also rewarded with a place in the Team of the Year for the second consecutive season.<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_player_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_player-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9312:_Final_season_in_France"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201112:_Final_season_in_France">201112: Final season in France</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 201112: Final season in France">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard_2011.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Eden_Hazard_2011.jpg/170px-Eden_Hazard_2011.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="289" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Eden_Hazard_2011.jpg/255px-Eden_Hazard_2011.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Eden_Hazard_2011.jpg/340px-Eden_Hazard_2011.jpg 2x" data-file-width="471" data-file-height="800" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard_2011.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard taking a <a href="/wiki/Corner_kick" title="Corner kick">corner kick</a> for Lille in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>Ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_in_French_football" title="201112 in French football">201112 season</a>, Hazard switched to the number 10 shirt.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> In Lille's first competitive match of the season against Marseille in the <a href="/wiki/2011_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2011 Trophée des Champions">2011 Trophée des Champions</a>, Hazard scored the team's second goal, which put Lille up 20. Marseille would later come back to win the match 54.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> On 10 September, he scored two goals in a 31 away victory against Saint-Étienne.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> Fours days after, Hazard made his <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> debut in a 22 group stage draw with Russian club <a href="/wiki/PFC_CSKA_Moscow" title="PFC CSKA Moscow">CSKA Moscow</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In Lille's next league match following his Champions League debut, he converted a penalty in a 22 draw with Sochaux.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Three days after, Hazard scored the equalizing goal in a 11 draw against Bordeaux.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> After going over two months without scoring a league goal, on 3 December, Hazard came on as a substitute and scored the match-winning goal in a win over <a href="/wiki/AC_Ajaccio" title="AC Ajaccio">Ajaccio</a> converting a penaltydescribed as an "<a href="/wiki/Anton%C3%ADn_Panenka" title="Antonín Panenka">Antonín Panenka</a>-style chipped penalty".<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> Two days later, Hazard was among several players nominated for <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a>'s <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">Team of the Year</a> for the 2011 calendar year.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> In Lille's final match before the winter break, Hazard tied his career-high for league goals in a season by scoring the team's third goal in a 44 draw with Nice.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> After scoring the goal, Hazard celebrated by paying tribute to Molami Bokoto, a former Lille youth academy player who had died a day prior.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> On 3 March, Hazard scored both goals in a 22 draw with Auxerre.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 18 March, Hazard scored a goal and assisted two others in a 40 win over local rivals Valenciennes.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> In Lille's next match against <a href="/wiki/Evian_Thonon_Gaillard_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Evian Thonon Gaillard F.C.">Evian</a>, Hazard converted a penalty and assisted a goal by <a href="/wiki/Dimitri_Payet" title="Dimitri Payet">Dimitri Payet</a> in a 30 win.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> The following week, on 1 April, Hazard converted a first-half penalty and later assisted another Payet goal to cap a 21 victory over Toulouse.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> On 15 April, Hazard marked his 100 consecutive Ligue 1 appearance, which to date, is the longest current run in the French top flight, by scoring a goal and assisting on another in a 41 win over Ajaccio.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> On 29 April, in a vital league fixture against PSG, he converted his ninth penalty of the season to draw the match at 11 cancelling out a goal from <a href="/wiki/Javier_Pastore" title="Javier Pastore">Javier Pastore</a>. Hazard later contributed to Lille's game-winning goal after delivering a <i><a href="/wiki/Rabona" title="Rabona">rabona</a></i>-style cross into the box, which was laid onto the path of striker <a href="/wiki/Nolan_Roux" title="Nolan Roux">Nolan Roux</a> who, subsequently, converted the goal to give Lille a 21 win.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 28 April, for the third consecutive season, Hazard was nominated for the Player of the Year award.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> Two weeks later, he was awarded the prestigious honour ahead of the likes of <a href="/wiki/Olivier_Giroud" title="Olivier Giroud">Olivier Giroud</a> and <a href="/wiki/Youn%C3%A8s_Belhanda" title="Younès Belhanda">Younès Belhanda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> After capturing the award, Hazard became the second player in the awards' history after former PSG striker <a href="/wiki/Pauleta" title="Pauleta">Pauleta</a> to achieve the honour in consecutive seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> He was also included in the Team of the Year for the third straight season. On 20 May, Hazard appeared in his final match as a Lille player against Nancy, the club he had made his professional debut against. In the match, Hazard scored his first <a href="/wiki/List_of_Ligue_1_hat-tricks" title="List of Ligue 1 hat-tricks">hat-trick</a> in a 41 win.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chelsea">Chelsea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Chelsea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 4 June 2012, Chelsea officially confirmed on its website that the club had agreed terms with Lille for the transfer of Hazard. The midfielder agreed personal terms with the club and passed a medical examination. The transfer fee was reported to be priced at £32 million.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> Upon signing, Hazard told the club's official website "I'm delighted to finally arrive here. It's a wonderful club and I can't wait to get started".<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> Hazard was given the number 17, which was previously worn by <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Bosingwa" title="José Bosingwa">José Bosingwa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9313:_Debut_season_and_first_trophy"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201213:_Debut_season_and_first_trophy">201213: Debut season and first trophy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 201213: Debut season and first trophy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard_2012.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Eden_Hazard_2012.jpg/240px-Eden_Hazard_2012.jpg" decoding="async" width="240" height="180" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Eden_Hazard_2012.jpg/360px-Eden_Hazard_2012.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Eden_Hazard_2012.jpg/480px-Eden_Hazard_2012.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3648" data-file-height="2736" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard_2012.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard preparing to take a corner kick in September 2012</div></div></div>
<p>On 12 August 2012, Hazard made his debut for Chelsea in the <a href="/wiki/2012_FA_Community_Shield" title="2012 FA Community Shield">2012 FA Community Shield</a> against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>, which ended in a 32 defeat at <a href="/wiki/Villa_Park" title="Villa Park">Villa Park</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> A week later, he made his league debut against <a href="/wiki/Wigan_Athletic_F.C." title="Wigan Athletic F.C.">Wigan Athletic</a> at the <a href="/wiki/DW_Stadium" title="DW Stadium">DW Stadium</a>. In the contest, Hazard provided the assist for <a href="/wiki/Branislav_Ivanovi%C4%87" title="Branislav Ivanovi">Branislav Ivanovi</a>'s opening goal and, minutes later, won a penalty, which <a href="/wiki/Frank_Lampard" title="Frank Lampard">Frank Lampard</a> converted, earning his side a 20 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> He made his <a href="/wiki/Stamford_Bridge_(stadium)" title="Stamford Bridge (stadium)">Stamford Bridge</a> debut in the team's next fixture, against <a href="/wiki/Reading_F.C." title="Reading F.C.">Reading</a> on 22 August, he won another penalty from which Lampard converted. Hazard also assisted goals by <a href="/wiki/Gary_Cahill" title="Gary Cahill">Gary Cahill</a> and Branislav Ivanovi as Chelsea won 42 at Stamford Bridge.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Hazard scored his first goal as a Chelsea player in a league match against <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> after scoring a penalty. Chelsea won the match 20.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard made his <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201213 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> debut for Chelsea in the team's opening group stage game against <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>  During December, he scored in back-to-back games, in a 51 away victory over <a href="/wiki/Leeds_United_F.C." title="Leeds United F.C.">Leeds United</a> in the <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">League Cup</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> and an 80 league win against <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> In January 2013, Hazard scored a goal with his left-foot from 25 yards in Chelsea's 40 win over <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a>, as Chelsea inflicted the first home defeat of the season on Stoke.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> He scored again in the following game, with an impressive strike from the edge of the area in a 22 draw at home to <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:29%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">I've said to him he has got absolutely everything. He's only 22, he has the world at his feet and with the way he's playing and the ability he has on the ball, he is scaring the life out of people.</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><a href="/wiki/Frank_Lampard" title="Frank Lampard">Frank Lampard</a> on the 22-year-old Eden Hazard in March 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-Lampard_compare_Hazard_to_Zola_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lampard_compare_Hazard_to_Zola-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 23 January, he was sent off in the <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">Football League Cup</a> semi-final second leg game against <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea City</a> for kicking a ball out from underneath a <a href="/wiki/Ball_boy#Association_football" title="Ball boy">ball boy</a> who was lying on it in order to waste time. Chelsea went on to lose the tie 20.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> Thereafter, he told Chelsea TV that he "apologised and the boy apologised" to each other.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> It was later revealed that the 17-year-old ball boy had planned before the game to deliberately waste time.<sup id="cite_ref-Hazard2_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hazard2-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> On 9 February, he scored on his return from suspension in a 41 win at home against <a href="/wiki/Wigan_Athletic_F.C." title="Wigan Athletic F.C.">Wigan Athletic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 21 February, Hazard came on as a substitute against <a href="/wiki/Sparta_Prague" class="mw-redirect" title="Sparta Prague">Sparta Prague</a> and scored an individual goal in stoppage time, to send Chelsea through to the last 16 on a 21 aggregate score.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> Again Hazard came off the bench to make an impact for Chelsea, scoring a goal and providing an assist to <a href="/wiki/Ramires" title="Ramires">Ramires</a>, as the Blues came back 20 down to salvage a 22 draw against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in the quarter-finals of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_FA_Cup" title="201213 FA Cup">FA Cup</a> on 10 March, setting up a replay at Stamford Bridge.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> On 17 March, Hazard put in a Man of the Match performance at Stamford Bridge in a 20 victory over <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a>, assisting Lampard's 200th Chelsea goal, then scoring a solo goal.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> On 11 May, at Villa Park, Hazard was the provider of Lampard's brace against Aston Villa, which enabled Lampard to break <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Tambling" title="Bobby Tambling">Bobby Tambling</a>'s all-time goal scoring record for Chelsea. However an injury picked up in the same game ruled him out of the <a href="/wiki/2013_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2013 UEFA Europa League Final">Europa League Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> Hazard ended his debut campaign at Chelsea with 13 goals in all competitions.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9315:_Premier_League_winner_and_individual_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201315:_Premier_League_winner_and_individual_success">201315: Premier League winner and individual success</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 201315: Premier League winner and individual success">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>One of Chelsea's first games of the season was against <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2013_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2013 UEFA Super Cup">2013 UEFA Super Cup</a>, where Hazard played a vital role in the buildup to the first goal and scored the second, but went on to an eventual 54 defeat in the penalty shoot-out.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> In October 2013, Hazard, as a substitute, scored the game-clinching goal in a 31 <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> clash against <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Norwich City">Norwich City</a> at <a href="/wiki/Carrow_Road" title="Carrow Road">Carrow Road</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> before scoring twice and assisting <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Eto%27o" title="Samuel Eto&#39;o">Samuel Eto'o</a>'s first Chelsea goal in a comprehensive defeat of <a href="/wiki/Cardiff_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Cardiff City">Cardiff City</a> in the same competition.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> Hazard netted his fifth goal of the season against <a href="/wiki/FC_Schalke_04" title="FC Schalke 04">Schalke</a> in a crucial 03 <a href="/wiki/2013-14_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" class="mw-redirect" title="2013-14 UEFA Champions League group stage">Champions League Group stage</a> win.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> In October, Hazard was part of the 23-man shortlist of players nominated for the prestigious <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Ballon_d%27Or" title="FIFA Ballon d&#39;Or">FIFA Ballon d'Or</a>, awarded to the player who is voted the men's world footballer of the year.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard%2713-14.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Eden_Hazard%2713-14.JPG/150px-Eden_Hazard%2713-14.JPG" decoding="async" width="150" height="208" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Eden_Hazard%2713-14.JPG/225px-Eden_Hazard%2713-14.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Eden_Hazard%2713-14.JPG/300px-Eden_Hazard%2713-14.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1416" data-file-height="1963" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard%2713-14.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard playing against <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K._(football)" title="Galatasaray S.K. (football)">Galatasaray</a> in a <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201314 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> match in February 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 9 November, Hazard created Chelsea's first goal against <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a>, which was scored by Eto'o. Later in the match Chelsea went 21 down, but Hazard scored a last minute penalty to clinch a point for his team.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> On 4 December, Hazard scored a brace in a 43 away victory over <a href="/wiki/Sunderland_A.F.C." title="Sunderland A.F.C.">Sunderland</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> with coach <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> claiming that Hazard delivered his best performance of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> Sunderland manager <a href="/wiki/Gus_Poyet" title="Gus Poyet">Gus Poyet</a> also praised Hazard for his individual impact on the game, saying he was "outstanding. He was unplayable, as a manager I haven't come up against anyone like that."<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:20%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">I keep saying he has to improve. He needs to have his feet on the ground. Ronaldo and Messi are Ronaldo and Messi. Eden Hazard is probably the best young player in the world with legs to go there, but give him time</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> on the 23-year-old Eden Hazard in February 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 26 December, Hazard scored the only goal in Chelsea's 10 victory over <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> In Chelsea's next league match, Hazard scored a goal from 25 yards during Chelsea's 21 victory over <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> After Hazard maintained his excellent form in Chelsea's 10 victory over Manchester City at the Etihad Stadium on 3 February 2014, Mourinho declared Hazard as the best young footballer in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> Hazard scored his first <a href="/wiki/List_of_Premier_League_hat-tricks" title="List of Premier League hat-tricks">Premier League hat-trick</a> against Newcastle United at Stamford Bridge on 8 February.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 April, Hazard won the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Young_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Young Player of the Year">PFA Young Player of the Year</a> award and finished as the runner-up to <a href="/wiki/Luis_Su%C3%A1rez" title="Luis Suárez">Luis Suárez</a> for the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a> award for his fine attacking performances under José Mourinho.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> After Chelsea's Champions League exit against <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>, Hazard claimed that Chelsea are only set up to counter-attack.<sup id="cite_ref-sacrifice_155-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sacrifice-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> Mourinho responded by saying that Hazard "is not so mentally ready" to help his defence, blaming him for the first goal scored by the opponents.<sup id="cite_ref-sacrifice_155-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sacrifice-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> In May, Hazard was voted Chelsea's Player of the Year in his second season at Stamford Bridge.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon <a href="/wiki/Juan_Mata" title="Juan Mata">Juan Mata</a>'s departure from the club in January, Hazard was handed the number 10 shirt for Chelsea ahead of the 201415 season.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> On 5 October, he won a penalty against Arsenal after being fouled by <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Koscielny" title="Laurent Koscielny">Laurent Koscielny</a>, and then converted it himself past <a href="/wiki/Wojciech_Szcz%C4%99sny" title="Wojciech Szczsny">Wojciech Szczsny</a> to open a 20 victory which made Chelsea the last unbeaten team in the league.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> In doing so, he maintained his 100% penalty record out of 16 penalties. He also became the only player in Europe who has taken more than 15 penalties and scored all of them.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_1_lLiverpool_0_(2-1_agg)_Capital_One_Cup_semi_final_2nd_leg_On_our_way_to_Wembley!_(16203132608)_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Chelsea_1_lLiverpool_0_%282-1_agg%29_Capital_One_Cup_semi_final_2nd_leg_On_our_way_to_Wembley%21_%2816203132608%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/150px-Chelsea_1_lLiverpool_0_%282-1_agg%29_Capital_One_Cup_semi_final_2nd_leg_On_our_way_to_Wembley%21_%2816203132608%29_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="223" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Chelsea_1_lLiverpool_0_%282-1_agg%29_Capital_One_Cup_semi_final_2nd_leg_On_our_way_to_Wembley%21_%2816203132608%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/225px-Chelsea_1_lLiverpool_0_%282-1_agg%29_Capital_One_Cup_semi_final_2nd_leg_On_our_way_to_Wembley%21_%2816203132608%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Chelsea_1_lLiverpool_0_%282-1_agg%29_Capital_One_Cup_semi_final_2nd_leg_On_our_way_to_Wembley%21_%2816203132608%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/300px-Chelsea_1_lLiverpool_0_%282-1_agg%29_Capital_One_Cup_semi_final_2nd_leg_On_our_way_to_Wembley%21_%2816203132608%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="997" data-file-height="1482" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_1_lLiverpool_0_(2-1_agg)_Capital_One_Cup_semi_final_2nd_leg_On_our_way_to_Wembley!_(16203132608)_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard playing against Liverpool in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Football_League_Cup" title="201415 Football League Cup">League Cup</a> <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Football_League_Cup#Semi-finals" title="201415 Football League Cup">semi-finals</a> in January 2015</div></div></div><p>
His first goals of the <a href="/wiki/2014-15_UEFA_Champions_League" class="mw-redirect" title="2014-15 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> campaign came on 21 October, netting from the penalty-spot and from open play in a 60 home win over <a href="/wiki/NK_Maribor" title="NK Maribor">Maribor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup> On 5 November, away to the Slovene team, he earned an 85th-minute penalty but had it saved by <a href="/wiki/Jasmin_Handanovi%C4%87" title="Jasmin Handanovi">Jasmin Handanovi</a> in a 11 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> Hazard opened the scoring in Chelsea's 20 win over Hull on 13 December, with the goal being only the second headed one of his entire career.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> The header came as a surprised for many, even Mourinho, who stated: "That he scored in the air, I was surprised. He jumps a lot but normally he closes his eyes. So I was surprised, but very good goal."<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup></p><div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:20%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">On his day, nobody can stop him. He has such great quality on the ball. He can create something from nothing and this is the sign of a special player.</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""><a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a> on the 24-year-old Eden Hazard in March 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 12 February 2015, Hazard signed a new five-and-a-half-year contract with Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> After signing, Hazard said: "I've signed a new contract and I'm very happy because I'm playing for one of the best clubs in the world."<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> He played the full 90 minutes in the club's victory in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Football_League_Cup_Final" title="2015 Football League Cup Final">League Cup Final</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a> on 1 March, a 20 win over Tottenham.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 18 April, Hazard scored the only goal in a home win over <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>, after he latched on to Oscar's backheel pass to score past <a href="/wiki/David_de_Gea" title="David de Gea">David de Gea</a>. He was voted Man of the Match thereafter for his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> As a result of Hazard's impressive performances throughout the 201415 campaign, his manager declared him "one of the top three players in the world".<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> On 26 April, Hazard was recognised as the best player of the season among his peers, winning the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> A week later, he scored the only goal as Chelsea defeated Crystal Palace to win their first Premier League title since 2010. He won a penalty after being fouled by <a href="/wiki/James_McArthur" title="James McArthur">James McArthur</a>, and took it himself, heading in the rebound after it was saved by <a href="/wiki/Juli%C3%A1n_Speroni" title="Julián Speroni">Julián Speroni</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 26 May, Hazard was voted as Chelsea's <a href="/wiki/List_of_Chelsea_F.C._players" title="List of Chelsea F.C. players">Player of the Year</a> for the second year in a row. There are only four other players that have done it in the past; <a href="/wiki/Juan_Mata" title="Juan Mata">Juan Mata</a>, <a href="/wiki/Frank_Lampard" title="Frank Lampard">Frank Lampard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ray_Wilkins" title="Ray Wilkins">Ray Wilkins</a>, and <a href="/wiki/John_Hollins" title="John Hollins">John Hollins</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard_-_DK-Chel15_(6).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Eden_Hazard_-_DK-Chel15_%286%29.jpg/170px-Eden_Hazard_-_DK-Chel15_%286%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="211" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Eden_Hazard_-_DK-Chel15_%286%29.jpg/255px-Eden_Hazard_-_DK-Chel15_%286%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Eden_Hazard_-_DK-Chel15_%286%29.jpg/340px-Eden_Hazard_-_DK-Chel15_%286%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="457" data-file-height="567" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard_-_DK-Chel15_(6).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard playing against <a href="/wiki/FC_Dynamo_Kyiv" title="FC Dynamo Kyiv">Dynamo Kyiv</a> in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> in October 2015</div></div></div>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316:_Year_of_scrutiny"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201516:_Year_of_scrutiny">201516: Year of scrutiny</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 201516: Year of scrutiny">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Hazard endured a difficult start to the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Chelsea_F.C._season" title="201516 Chelsea F.C. season">201516 season</a>, missing a penalty in the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage#Group_G" title="201516 UEFA Champions League group stage">Champions League group stage</a> against <a href="/wiki/Maccabi_Tel_Aviv_F.C." title="Maccabi Tel Aviv F.C.">Maccabi Tel Aviv</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> On 27 October, in the fourth round of the League Cup away to Stoke, Hazard was the only player to miss in Chelsea's penalty shootout elimination, his attempt being saved by <a href="/wiki/Jack_Butland" title="Jack Butland">Jack Butland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> Hazard endured a 2,358-minute scoreless run across 30 matches until 31 January 2016, when he scored from the penalty spot, his 50th goal for Chelsea in all competitions, in a 51 win over <a href="/wiki/Milton_Keynes_Dons_F.C." title="Milton Keynes Dons F.C.">Milton Keynes Dons</a> in the fourth round of the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In February, Hazard was scrutinised when he said it would "be difficult to say no" to a move to Paris Saint-Germain.<sup id="cite_ref-riach_176-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-riach-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> He remained scoreless in the league until 23 April, when he recorded two goals in a 41 victory at <a href="/wiki/AFC_Bournemouth" title="AFC Bournemouth">Bournemouth</a>; after the result, interim manager <a href="/wiki/Guus_Hiddink" title="Guus Hiddink">Guus Hiddink</a> insisted that Hazard would remain at Chelsea by next season.<sup id="cite_ref-riach_176-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-riach-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> For the second consecutive campaign, Hazard scored the goal that decided the Premier League; he came on as a substitute at home to Tottenham on 2 May, and scored an equaliser as Chelsea came from 20 down at half-time to draw. The result meant <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> won the title at Tottenham's expense.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> On 11 May 2016, Hazard scored his fourth and final league goal of the season against Liverpool, although Chelsea were unable to hold on to the lead, with fellow countryman <a href="/wiki/Christian_Benteke" title="Christian Benteke">Christian Benteke</a> scoring in extra time as the match finished in a 11 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9318:_Premier_League_winner_and_first_FA_Cup_win"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201618:_Premier_League_winner_and_first_FA_Cup_win">201618: Premier League winner and first FA Cup win</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 201618: Premier League winner and first FA Cup win">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 15 August, in Chelsea's opening Premier League match of the season, Hazard scored a penalty in a 21 win over <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup> Hazard recorded a total of 81 touches throughout the game, and his performance earned him the Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> On 27 August, Hazard contributed another Man of the Match display in the 30 victory over <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a>, scoring the opener in the ninth minute.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> After voting ended on 5 September, Hazard received the most votes from the public poll, 41%, for the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Player of the Month">Premier League Player of the Month</a> award<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> although <a href="/wiki/Raheem_Sterling" title="Raheem Sterling">Raheem Sterling</a> was later named the Player of the Month by a Premier League panel.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
