<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:197px;"><a href="/wiki/File:EdenHazardDecember_2016.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/EdenHazardDecember_2016.jpg/195px-EdenHazardDecember_2016.jpg" decoding="async" width="195" height="221" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/EdenHazardDecember_2016.jpg/292px-EdenHazardDecember_2016.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/EdenHazardDecember_2016.jpg/389px-EdenHazardDecember_2016.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2303" data-file-height="2614" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:EdenHazardDecember_2016.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard during a Premier League game against <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion" class="mw-redirect" title="West Bromwich Albion">West Bromwich Albion</a> in December 2016</div></div></div>
<p>On 15 October, Hazard, along with <a href="/wiki/Diego_Costa" title="Diego Costa">Diego Costa</a> dedicated their goals to <a href="/wiki/Willian_(footballer,_born_1988)" title="Willian (footballer, born 1988)">Willian</a>, whose mother had died earlier that week, in the 30 victory over the champions, Leicester City.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> On 23 October, he scored his fourth goal of the season in a 40 win over former Chelsea manager, José Mourinho's <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>, equalling the number of league goals he managed in the previous season.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> Hazard continued his excellent form, scoring the first goal and assisting the second in Chelsea's 20 win over <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a> on 30 October. This marked the first time that he had scored in three consecutive Premier League games.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> His run of form continued into the next match as he scored two goals and assisted another in Chelsea's 50 win against <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> at Stamford Bridge on 5 November. Hazard's performance against Everton earned him another Man of the Match award, his third in a row in the Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup> On 18 November, Hazard was named the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Player of the Month">Premier League Player of the Month</a> for October.<sup id="cite_ref-Premier_League_188-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Premier_League-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 26 December, Hazard led the Blues to their twelfth consecutive league victory, a new club record, in the 30 victory over <a href="/wiki/A.F.C._Bournemouth" class="mw-redirect" title="A.F.C. Bournemouth">Bournemouth</a>. He also converted a penalty for his 50th Premier League goal, making him the sixth Chelsea player to achieve this feat.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> On 20 April 2017, Hazard was named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> for the fourth time in his five seasons at Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-PFA1617_190-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PFA1617-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> Two days later, he scored after coming on as a substitute in Chelsea's 42 <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_FA_Cup" title="201617 FA Cup">FA Cup</a> semi-final victory over rivals <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hazard_v_Newcastle.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Hazard_v_Newcastle.jpg/220px-Hazard_v_Newcastle.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="172" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Hazard_v_Newcastle.jpg/330px-Hazard_v_Newcastle.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Hazard_v_Newcastle.jpg/440px-Hazard_v_Newcastle.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2662" data-file-height="2081" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hazard_v_Newcastle.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard playing against <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United" class="mw-redirect" title="Newcastle United">Newcastle United</a> in the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> in January 2018</div></div></div>
<p>At the beginning of the summer, Hazard suffered an ankle injury in training during international duty.<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> The injury ruled him out for 6 to 8 weeks; missing the entire preseason and the Premier League opener.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> On 25 August, Hazard returned to action, playing 75 minutes for the <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C._Under-23s_and_Academy" title="Chelsea F.C. Under-23s and Academy">Chelsea U23</a> side.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> On 28 October, Hazard scored his first league goal of the season in a 10 win against Bournemouth in the Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> On 3 January 2018, Hazard scored in a 22 draw with <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C.%E2%80%93Chelsea_F.C._rivalry" title="Arsenal F.C.Chelsea F.C. rivalry">rivals</a> Arsenal.<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup> Two goals against <a href="/wiki/Brighton_%26_Hove_Albion" class="mw-redirect" title="Brighton &amp; Hove Albion">Brighton &amp; Hove Albion</a> on 20 January made it 100 league goals in his career. Hazard's double helped Chelsea to a 40 win at <a href="/wiki/Falmer_Stadium" title="Falmer Stadium">Falmer Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup> On 12 February, Hazard scored a double in a 30 win over West Bromwich Albion.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2018_FA_Cup_Final" title="2018 FA Cup Final">2018 FA Cup Final</a> on 19 May, Hazard won a penalty which he converted, sending it low to the right past Manchester United goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/David_de_Gea" title="David de Gea">David de Gea</a> for the only goal of the game.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319:_Final_season_in_England"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201819:_Final_season_in_England">201819: Final season in England</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 201819: Final season in England">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_vs._Arsenal,_29_May_2019_30.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Chelsea_vs._Arsenal%2C_29_May_2019_30.jpg/220px-Chelsea_vs._Arsenal%2C_29_May_2019_30.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Chelsea_vs._Arsenal%2C_29_May_2019_30.jpg/330px-Chelsea_vs._Arsenal%2C_29_May_2019_30.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9b/Chelsea_vs._Arsenal%2C_29_May_2019_30.jpg/440px-Chelsea_vs._Arsenal%2C_29_May_2019_30.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1050" data-file-height="700" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_vs._Arsenal,_29_May_2019_30.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard wearing his <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> winners medal in May 2019</div></div></div>
<p>Hazard scored on his first start of the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Chelsea_F.C._season" title="201819 Chelsea F.C. season">201819 season</a>, converting a penalty in a 21 win against <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United" class="mw-redirect" title="Newcastle United">Newcastle United</a> on 26 August.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup> On 15 September, Hazard scored a hat-trick in a 41 win over <a href="/wiki/Cardiff_City_F.C." title="Cardiff City F.C.">Cardiff City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup> He came off the bench to give Chelsea a 21 come-from-behind win over <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_FC" class="mw-redirect" title="Liverpool FC">Liverpool</a> in the third round of the <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> at Anfield on 26 September. It was his sixth goal in seven appearances to start the season.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> In the next fixture, against Liverpool in the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a>, he made it seven goals in eight games, opening the scoring in a 11 draw at <a href="/wiki/Stamford_Bridge_(stadium)" title="Stamford Bridge (stadium)">Stamford Bridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> On 16 December, Hazard scored and assisted a goal for <a href="/wiki/Pedro_(footballer,_born_1987)" title="Pedro (footballer, born 1987)">Pedro</a> as Chelsea won 21 away to Brighton &amp; Hove Albion in the league, before coming off the bench to send Chelsea through to the EFL Cup semi-final at the expense of Bournemouth three days later.<sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup> He scored both goals in a 21 Boxing Day win against <a href="/wiki/Watford_FC" class="mw-redirect" title="Watford FC">Watford</a> at <a href="/wiki/Vicarage_Road" title="Vicarage Road">Vicarage Road</a>, the first of which was his 100th Blues and 150th career club goal.<sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 8 April 2019, Hazard scored a solo goal against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a> which would be voted as <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Goal_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Goal of the Month">Premier League Goal of the Month</a> for April.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup> On 9 May 2019, Hazard scored the decisive penalty in a 43 shootout win over <a href="/wiki/Eintracht_Frankfurt" title="Eintracht Frankfurt">Eintracht Frankfurt</a> at Stamford Bridge to send Chelsea to the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2019 UEFA Europa League Final">Europa League Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup> His tally of 15 assists for the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Premier_League" title="201819 Premier League">201819 Premier League</a> season saw him win the Premier League's <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Playmaker_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Playmaker of the Season">Playmaker of the Season</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> Hazard joined Thierry Henry, Matt Le Tissier and Eric Cantona to become the 4th player in premier league history to record at least 15 goals and 15 assists in a premier league season.<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup> On 29 May, Chelsea won the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Europa_League" title="201819 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a> following a 41 win over Arsenal in the <a href="/wiki/2019_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2019 UEFA Europa League Final">final</a>, in which Hazard scored twice, also assisting Pedro's goal.<sup id="cite_ref-2019UEL_211-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2019UEL-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup> After the match, Hazard suggested that it probably was the last time he would play for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Madrid">Real Madrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Real Madrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Transfer">Transfer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Transfer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:FC_RB_Salzburg_versus_Real_Madrid_(Testspiel,_7._August_2019)_15.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/FC_RB_Salzburg_versus_Real_Madrid_%28Testspiel%2C_7._August_2019%29_15.jpg/220px-FC_RB_Salzburg_versus_Real_Madrid_%28Testspiel%2C_7._August_2019%29_15.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="365" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/FC_RB_Salzburg_versus_Real_Madrid_%28Testspiel%2C_7._August_2019%29_15.jpg/330px-FC_RB_Salzburg_versus_Real_Madrid_%28Testspiel%2C_7._August_2019%29_15.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/FC_RB_Salzburg_versus_Real_Madrid_%28Testspiel%2C_7._August_2019%29_15.jpg/440px-FC_RB_Salzburg_versus_Real_Madrid_%28Testspiel%2C_7._August_2019%29_15.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1186" data-file-height="1968" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:FC_RB_Salzburg_versus_Real_Madrid_(Testspiel,_7._August_2019)_15.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard during a preseason match with Real Madrid in 2019</div></div></div>
<p>On 7 June 2019, <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> announced on their website that Hazard would be signing for them for the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="201920 Real Madrid CF season">201920 season</a>. He signed a contract until 30 June 2024 for a reported fee of 100 million, which could rise to 146.1 million due to additional fees, on a deal worth £400,000 per week.<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup> Hazard was formally unveiled in front of 50,000 fans on 13 June at the <a href="/wiki/Santiago_Bernab%C3%A9u_Stadium" title="Santiago Bernabéu Stadium">Santiago Bernabéu</a>. Hazard became Madrid's most expensive player after <a href="/wiki/Gareth_Bale" title="Gareth Bale">Gareth Bale</a> who was signed for 101 million in 2013. Should any of the variables be met, Hazard would become Madrid's most expensive player in their history.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup> Hazard was presented at the Bernabéu without a number on his jersey; he had been wearing the number 10 for both Chelsea and Belgium for a number of years, and admitted that he had asked <a href="/wiki/Luka_Modri%C4%87" title="Luka Modri">Luka Modri</a> for the number at Madrid but Modri refused to give it away.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup> Nearly two months later, Madrid confirmed that Hazard will wear the number 7, previously worn by club legends <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_(footballer)" title="Raúl (footballer)">Raúl González</a> and <a href="/wiki/Emilio_Butrague%C3%B1o" title="Emilio Butragueño">Emilio Butragueño</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon signing with Real Madrid, Hazard said "I've dreamt about this since I was little, I always supported Real Madrid" and described it as "a true honour." He listed manager <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a> as a defining factor in making the move, as he had always been an admirer of him.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320:_Spain_debut.2C_league_winner.2C_injuries"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201920:_Spain_debut,_league_winner,_injuries">201920: Spain debut, league winner, injuries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 201920: Spain debut, league winner, injuries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Hazard made his debut on 14 September 2019, coming on as a substitute in a 32 victory over <a href="/wiki/Levante_UD" title="Levante UD">Levante</a> in <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_La_Liga" title="201920 La Liga">La Liga</a> at the Bernabeu.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup> On 5 October, he scored his first competitive goal for Los Blancos, right before half time against <a href="/wiki/Granada_CF" title="Granada CF">Granada</a> in his first home league start. In the second half, he also got his first assist which was to Modri in an eventual 42 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup> On 26 November, Hazard suffered an ankle injury against Paris Saint-Germain in the Champions League group stage after a rash challenge by Belgium teammate <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Meunier" title="Thomas Meunier">Thomas Meunier</a>. He was unable to continue and was substituted moments later.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup> A day later, Madrid's medical team suggested the ankle injury was "an external bruise" expected to keep Hazard on the sidelines for just 10 days.<sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup> But one week later, further tests by the medical team revealed he suffered an "incomplete external micro fracture" in his right ankle, with no set return date.<sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup> Hazard went on to miss 16 Madrid matches across four competitions, which included the first <a href="/wiki/El_Cl%C3%A1sico" title="El Clásico">El Clásico</a> of the season, the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="201920 Supercopa de España">Supercopa de España</a> victory in <a href="/wiki/Jeddah" title="Jeddah">Jeddah</a> and the entire <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Copa_del_Rey" title="201920 Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> campaign which ended with a quarter-final exit to <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Sociedad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 16 February, Hazard made his return from injury and started against Celta Vigo in La Liga. He earned a penalty after being fouled by Celta's goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Rub%C3%A9n_Blanco" title="Rubén Blanco">Rubén Blanco</a> in the area, which <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ramos" title="Sergio Ramos">Sergio Ramos</a> converted to make it 21 to the hosts. Hazard went off to a standing ovation in the 73rd minute.<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup> Six days later, he suffered a "fracture to his right distal fibula" in his ankle during Madrid's 10 defeat against Levante and was forced off the pitch in the second half.<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup> The ankle injury forced Hazard to miss Madrid's two biggest games of the season, the Champions League Round of 16 clash against Manchester City and the second league El Clasico.<sup id="cite_ref-231" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-231">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup> In early March, Hazard's ankle was operated on in Dallas and he was expected to be out for three months, meaning his season would likely be over.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup> After La Liga restarted in June after a three-month hiatus due to the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Spain" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Spain">COVID-19 pandemic</a>, Hazard was available for selection.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup> On 14 June, in Madrid's first league game after the break, Hazard assisted Sergio Ramos against <a href="/wiki/SD_Eibar" title="SD Eibar">Eibar</a> in a 31 win at the <a href="/wiki/Alfredo_di_St%C3%A9fano_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Alfredo di Stéfano Stadium">Alfredo di Stéfano Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the season he had made 16 league appearances, as Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_La_Liga" title="201920 La Liga">201920 La Liga</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season_with_further_injuries"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="202021_season_with_further_injuries">202021 season with further injuries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 202021 season with further injuries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 31 October, Hazard scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="202021 Real Madrid CF season">202021 season</a> in Madrid's 41 home league win over <a href="/wiki/SD_Huesca" title="SD Huesca">Huesca</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup> On 25 November, he scored his first Champions League goal with Madrid in a 20 away win against <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth">Youth</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Youth">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Hazard played for various Belgian national youth teams, such as the <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_under-17_football_team" title="Belgium national under-17 football team">under-17</a> and <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_under-19_football_team" title="Belgium national under-19 football team">under-19</a> teams. With the under-17 team, he was a regular in the team making 17 appearances and scoring two goals. He played with the team in the <a href="/wiki/Toto_Cup" title="Toto Cup">Toto Cup</a>, a yearly international youth tournament held in Austria and, also, played in the <a href="/wiki/2007_UEFA_European_Under-17_Football_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="2007 UEFA European Under-17 Football Championship">2007 UEFA European Under-17 Football Championship</a>, which Belgium hosted. In the tournament, Hazard scored his only goal in the team's opening match against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_under-17_football_team" title="Netherlands national under-17 football team">Netherlands</a> converting a penalty in a 22 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup> The match was a homecoming for Hazard, as it was played in Tubize, where he spent part of his youth career.<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;239&#93;</a></sup> Throughout the tournament, Hazard impressed media and coaches, which led to many in Belgium comparing him to Belgian football legend <a href="/wiki/Enzo_Scifo" title="Enzo Scifo">Enzo Scifo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">&#91;240&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;241&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Belgium suffered elimination in the semi-finals of the competition, losing to <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_under-17_football_team" title="Spain national under-17 football team">Spain</a> 76 on penalties. Belgium were minutes away from a victory, courtesy of an own goal from David Rochela, which Hazard was particularly instrumental in, however <a href="/wiki/F.C._Barcelona" class="mw-redirect" title="F.C. Barcelona">Barcelona</a> striker <a href="/wiki/Bojan_Krki%C4%87" title="Bojan Krki">Bojan Krki</a> equalized for his nation to send the match into extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">&#91;243&#93;</a></sup> Due to finishing in third place at the tournament, Belgium qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2007_FIFA_U-17_World_Cup" title="2007 FIFA U-17 World Cup">2007 FIFA U-17 World Cup</a>, held in South Korea. Hazard was selected to participate and played in all three group stage matches, where Belgium were eliminated.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>After playing at the FIFA U-17 World Cup in August and September 2007, Hazard began earning call-ups to the under-19 team the following month in October. His first appearance came in a <a href="/wiki/2008_UEFA_European_Under-19_Football_Championship_qualification" class="mw-redirect" title="2008 UEFA European Under-19 Football Championship qualification">2008 UEFA European Under-19 Football Championship qualification</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a> coming on as a substitute in a 40 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">&#91;244&#93;</a></sup> He subsequently played in the next two group stage matches against <a href="/wiki/Iceland_national_football_team" title="Iceland national football team">Iceland</a> and <a href="/wiki/England_national_under-19_football_team" title="England national under-19 football team">England</a>. Belgium lost both matches.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">&#91;245&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246">&#91;246&#93;</a></sup> The negative results eliminated the country from the tournament. Due to being an underage player the previous year, Hazard was eligible for the under-19 team for the 200809 season. Due to his growing participation with Lille's first team, Hazard was only allowed to play in <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_European_Under-19_Football_Championship_qualification" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 UEFA European Under-19 Football Championship qualification">2009 UEFA European Under-19 Football Championship qualification</a> matches by his club and, as a result, missed the 2008 edition of the <a href="/wiki/Milk_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Milk Cup">Milk Cup</a>, which was held during Lille's preseason.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>On 7 October 2008, Hazard scored his first under-19 goal in the team's 50 victory over <a href="/wiki/Estonia_national_under-19_football_team" title="Estonia national under-19 football team">Estonia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247">&#91;247&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he scored a double in a 22 draw with <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">&#91;248&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_European_Under-19_Football_Championship_elite_qualification" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 UEFA European Under-19 Football Championship elite qualification">Elite Round</a>, Hazard led the team in goals scoring three. In the opening match against the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Republic of Ireland</a>, he scored the lone goal.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">&#91;249&#93;</a></sup> In the next match, Hazard was influential in the team's 50 thrashing of <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a> scoring a goal and assisting on two others.<sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">&#91;250&#93;</a></sup> In the team's final match, they faced <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a>. Belgium needed an outright victory to progress to the <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_European_Under-19_Football_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 UEFA European Under-19 Football Championship">2009 UEFA European Under-19 Football Championship</a>, but were eliminated from qualifying after drawing 11 with the Swiss, despite Hazard opening the scoring for Belgium in the 21st minute.<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251">&#91;251&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_senior">Early senior</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Early senior">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 18 November 2008, Hazard was called up to the <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium senior team</a>, for the first time, by manager <a href="/wiki/Ren%C3%A9_Vandereycken" title="René Vandereycken">René Vandereycken</a> for the team's match against <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg_national_football_team" title="Luxembourg national football team">Luxembourg</a>. Prior to making his national team debut with Belgium, Hazard was courted by <a href="/wiki/French_Football_Federation" title="French Football Federation">French Football Federation</a> officials who sought the player to play for the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France national team</a> as he had become eligible for French citizenship. Hazard did not respond to the courtship and later stated "Because of my presence in France for seven years, I feel 99% Belgian and 1% French, but the idea of French citizenship has never crossed my mind".<sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252">&#91;252&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard made his highly anticipated debut for Belgium in the match against Luxembourg coming on as a substitute in the 67th minute for <a href="/wiki/Wesley_Sonck" title="Wesley Sonck">Wesley Sonck</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253">&#91;253&#93;</a></sup> On his debut, Hazard became the eighth youngest international player in Belgian football history, at 17 years and 316 days.<sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254">&#91;254&#93;</a></sup> On 12 August 2009, after three consecutive substitute appearances with the team, he made his first start under coach <a href="/wiki/Franky_Vercauteren" title="Franky Vercauteren">Franky Vercauteren</a> in the team's 31 <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game#Association_football" title="Exhibition game">friendly</a> loss to the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic_national_football_team" title="Czech Republic national football team">Czech Republic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255">&#91;255&#93;</a></sup> Following the resignation of Vercauteren, he was replaced with manager <a href="/wiki/Dick_Advocaat" title="Dick Advocaat">Dick Advocaat</a>. Under Advocaat, Hazard became a starter in the team and, on 14 November 2009, played a full match for the first time in his international career. In the match, which was played against <a href="/wiki/Hungary_national_football_team" title="Hungary national football team">Hungary</a>, Hazard assisted two goals in a 30 win.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>In May 2010, Advocaat was replaced as manager by <a href="/wiki/Georges_Leekens" title="Georges Leekens">Georges Leekens</a>. After featuring as a starter in Leekens first three matches in charge, Hazard began appearing as a substitute for Belgium during the 201011 season. Leekens justified his benching of Hazard citing the players' domestic performance, which had been underwhelming at the time, while also admitting that Hazard displayed a lack of desire in training with the national team and often neglected his defensive duties during international matches.<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_leekens_64-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_leekens-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-256" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-256">&#91;256&#93;</a></sup> After appearing as a substitute in two straight matches, Hazard returned to the starting lineup for the team's November 2010 friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a>. In the match, which Belgium won 20, Hazard assisted the team's opening goal scored by <a href="/wiki/Romelu_Lukaku" title="Romelu Lukaku">Romelu Lukaku</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-257" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-257">&#91;257&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After featuring as a starter in the team's 11 draw with <a href="/wiki/Finland_national_football_team" title="Finland national football team">Finland</a> in February 2011, Hazard was relegated back to the substitute's bench for the team's important March 2011 <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying</a> matches as Leekens preferred <a href="/wiki/Nacer_Chadli" title="Nacer Chadli">Nacer Chadli</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mousa_Demb%C3%A9l%C3%A9_(footballer,_born_1987)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mousa Dembélé (footballer, born 1987)">Mousa Dembélé</a> on the wings.<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">&#91;258&#93;</a></sup> Following the matches, French media began questioning why Hazard was struggling to be appreciated in his home country, while, at the same time, was being praised in France.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">&#91;259&#93;</a></sup> Marc Wilmots, assistant coach of the national team, responded to the media reports stating "Some people only see Eden's qualities" and "the French press are sometimes blinded by his moments of magic".<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">&#91;260&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In Belgium's next competitive match against <a href="/wiki/Turkey_national_football_team" title="Turkey national football team">Turkey</a> on 3 June 2011, Hazard started the match, but was substituted out after 60 minutes. Disappointed with his performance and substitution, the midfielder retired to the locker room and was later spotted on television outside the stadium with his family eating a <a href="/wiki/Hamburger" title="Hamburger">hamburger</a> while the match was still ongoing.<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">&#91;261&#93;</a></sup> Following the episode, which has become known as <i>Burgergate</i> in Belgium,<sup id="cite_ref-262" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-262">&#91;262&#93;</a></sup> Hazard apologized for the defection, while Leekens attributed Hazard's response to the substitution as "a young player making a mistake".<sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263">&#91;263&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 August, Leekens announced that Hazard would be disciplined for his actions during the Turkey match and, as a result, would miss the team's 10 August friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Slovenia_national_football_team" title="Slovenia national football team">Slovenia</a>, as well as the team's Euro qualifying return match against Azerbaijan on 2 September and friendly against the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States men&#39;s national soccer team">United States</a> four days later.<sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264">&#91;264&#93;</a></sup> On 9 August, Hazard's management group issued a press release to the Belgian media. The release detailed Hazard's actions during the Turkey match, criticized the player's three-match suspension, as well as questioned Leekens constant criticism of Hazard.<sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265">&#91;265&#93;</a></sup> On 25 August, it was announced that Leekens had lifted Hazard's suspension and the midfielder was subsequently named in the team to play the September fixtures.<sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266">&#91;266&#93;</a></sup> Leekens decided to lift the suspension after having a meeting with Hazard that was organized by the player's agent.<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267">&#91;267&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 October 2011, nearly three years after his debut, Hazard scored his first international goal against <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan_national_football_team" title="Kazakhstan national football team">Kazakhstan</a> in a 41 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268">&#91;268&#93;</a></sup> The victory inserted Belgium into second-place position in its group in qualifying for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a> with the team needing a victory over <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> on 11 October to secure a place in the qualifying playoffs.<sup id="cite_ref-269" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-269">&#91;269&#93;</a></sup> In the match against Germany, Hazard played the entire match as Belgium failed to earn a place in the European Championship, losing 31 in <a href="/wiki/D%C3%BCsseldorf" title="Düsseldorf">Düsseldorf</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270">&#91;270&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_World_Cup_and_Euro_2016">2014 World Cup and Euro 2016</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 2014 World Cup and Euro 2016">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Hazard made nine appearances in the <i>Red Devils'</i> successful <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">2014 World Cup qualification</a> campaign, scoring twice.<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271">&#91;271&#93;</a></sup> The first of these came on 22 March against the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Macedonia_national_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of Macedonia national football team">Republic of Macedonia</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Philip_II_Arena" class="mw-redirect" title="Philip II Arena">Philip II Arena</a>, converting a penalty to conclude a 20 win after being fouled by <a href="/wiki/Aleksandar_Lazevski" title="Aleksandar Lazevski">Aleksandar Lazevski</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">&#91;272&#93;</a></sup> Three days later in the reverse fixture, he beat two defenders before scoring the only goal of the game.<sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">&#91;273&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 May 2014, Hazard was named in Belgium's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">&#91;274&#93;</a></sup> He assisted <a href="/wiki/Dries_Mertens" title="Dries Mertens">Dries Mertens</a>' winning goal in the team's first game of the tournament, a 21 win against <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> in <a href="/wiki/Belo_Horizonte" title="Belo Horizonte">Belo Horizonte</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">&#91;275&#93;</a></sup> In Belgium's second match, he assisted <a href="/wiki/Divock_Origi" title="Divock Origi">Divock Origi</a>'s 88th-minute goal, giving the Red Devils a 10 win over <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a> and qualifying them for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage" title="2014 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">knockout stage</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-bbc_276-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc-276">&#91;276&#93;</a></sup> eventually reaching the quarter-finals, where they were eliminated by <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277">&#91;277&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 June 2015, due to the suspension of regular skipper <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Kompany" title="Vincent Kompany">Vincent Kompany</a>, Hazard captained Belgium for the first time in a friendly against <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a>, scoring a penalty for Belgium's final goal in a 43 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-278" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-278">&#91;278&#93;</a></sup> He won another penalty in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying</a> match on 3 September when fouled by <a href="/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina_national_football_team" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina national football team">Bosnia and Herzegovina</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Ognjen_Vranje%C5%A1" title="Ognjen Vranje">Ognjen Vranje</a>, and converted it past his Chelsea clubmate <a href="/wiki/Asmir_Begovi%C4%87" title="Asmir Begovi">Asmir Begovi</a> to conclude Belgium's 31 comeback victory.<sup id="cite_ref-279" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-279">&#91;279&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he finished Mertens' cross with four minutes remaining, for the only goal in an away win over <a href="/wiki/Cyprus_national_football_team" title="Cyprus national football team">Cyprus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-280" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-280">&#91;280&#93;</a></sup> On 10 October, Hazard scored a spot-kick again after <a href="/wiki/%C3%93scar_Sonejee" title="Óscar Sonejee">Óscar Sonejee</a>'s handball, in a 41 win over <a href="/wiki/Andorra_national_football_team" title="Andorra national football team">Andorra</a> which sealed Belgium's qualification to the continental championship for the first time since co-hosting <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2000" title="UEFA Euro 2000">UEFA Euro 2000</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-281" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-281">&#91;281&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to the absence of Kompany, Hazard was named captain of Belgium for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a> finals.<sup id="cite_ref-282" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-282">&#91;282&#93;</a></sup> He scored a solo goal against <a href="/wiki/Hungary_national_football_team" title="Hungary national football team">Hungary</a> in the last 16, before Belgium were eliminated by <a href="/wiki/Wales_national_football_team" title="Wales national football team">Wales</a> in the quarter-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-283" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-283">&#91;283&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-284" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-284">&#91;284&#93;</a></sup> Alongside <a href="/wiki/Aaron_Ramsey" title="Aaron Ramsey">Aaron Ramsey</a>, he finished as the top assist provider of the tournament with four assists.<sup id="cite_ref-Euro_2016_stats_285-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Euro_2016_stats-285">&#91;285&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup">2018 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 2018 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:132px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard_2018.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Eden_Hazard_2018.jpg/130px-Eden_Hazard_2018.jpg" decoding="async" width="130" height="252" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Eden_Hazard_2018.jpg/195px-Eden_Hazard_2018.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Eden_Hazard_2018.jpg/260px-Eden_Hazard_2018.jpg 2x" data-file-width="596" data-file-height="1156" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Eden_Hazard_2018.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Appointed Belgium <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a>, Hazard led his nation to third place, the best finish in their history.<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286">&#91;286&#93;</a></sup></div></div></div>
<p>Hazard was appointed <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> of Belgium for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287">&#91;287&#93;</a></sup> In the first game against <a href="/wiki/Panama_national_football_team" title="Panama national football team">Panama</a>, he assisted the third goal of the match scored by Lukaku as Belgium won 30.<sup id="cite_ref-288" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-288">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup> He then scored twice (which included a penalty) in their second group stage victory against <a href="/wiki/Tunisia_national_football_team" title="Tunisia national football team">Tunisia</a>. His penalty goal in the 6th minute was the team's second quickest goal in the history of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-289" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-289">&#91;289&#93;</a></sup> Hazard was also selected the <a href="/wiki/Man-of-the-match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man-of-the-match">Man-of-the-match</a> after his impressive performance against Tunisia.<sup id="cite_ref-290" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-290">&#91;290&#93;</a></sup> In the final group match, Hazard did not play in Belgium's 10 victory over England as he, together with eight other starters in the previous two matches, were rested by Roberto Martinez.<sup id="cite_ref-291" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-291">&#91;291&#93;</a></sup> In Belgium's 32 victory over <a href="/wiki/Japan_national_football_team" title="Japan national football team">Japan</a> in the last 16, Hazard was instrumental in mounting a comeback from a two-goal deficit as Belgium became the first team in 52 years to come back from 02 down to win a World Cup knockout match.<sup id="cite_ref-292" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-292">&#91;292&#93;</a></sup> For his second consecutive game, Hazard was once again voted the Man of the match by FIFA sponsors, <a href="/wiki/Budweiser" title="Budweiser">Budweiser</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-293" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-293">&#91;293&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard was again in scintillating form in the quarter-finals as he helped lead Belgium to its second World Cup semi-final in their history with a 21 victory over five-time champions <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a>. In that game, Hazard set a World Cup record for successful <a href="/wiki/Dribbling" title="Dribbling">dribbles</a> completed in any World Cup game since 1966, with a 100% success rate in ten dribbles.<sup id="cite_ref-294" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-294">&#91;294&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-295" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-295">&#91;295&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-finals, which was a tight game, Belgium were defeated by eventual champions France 10 courtesy of Frenchman <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Umtiti" title="Samuel Umtiti">Samuel Umtiti</a>'s header and France's subsequent deep defense.<sup id="cite_ref-296" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-296">&#91;296&#93;</a></sup> On 14 July, Hazard's third Man of the match performance ensured victory for Belgium with his goal in the 82nd minute in a 20 victory against <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> in their <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup#Third_place_play-off" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">third-place play-off</a>, his nation's best ever World Cup finish.<sup id="cite_ref-297" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-297">&#91;297&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-298" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-298">&#91;298&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end of the 2018 FIFA World Cup on 15 July the FIFA Technical Study Group (TSG) selected Hazard as the second best player of the tournament, awarding him the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">Silver Ball</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_299-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-299">&#91;299&#93;</a></sup> In addition to his dribbling he scored three goals and provided two assists in total, as well as being selected the Man of the match on three different occasions  more than any other player.<sup id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_299-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-299">&#91;299&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2020">Euro 2020</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Euro 2020">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Hazard made his 100th cap for Belgium during the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2020 qualifying">Euro 2020 qualifiers</a> in a 20 away win against Cyprus in March 2019, scoring the second goal in that match.<sup id="cite_ref-300" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-300">&#91;300&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-301" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-301">&#91;301&#93;</a></sup> Hazard captained Belgium to become the first team to qualify for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020" title="UEFA Euro 2020">tournament</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-302" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-302">&#91;302&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Player_profile">Player profile</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Player profile">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hazard_taking_on_Howson.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Hazard_taking_on_Howson.jpg/250px-Hazard_taking_on_Howson.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Hazard_taking_on_Howson.jpg/375px-Hazard_taking_on_Howson.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Hazard_taking_on_Howson.jpg/500px-Hazard_taking_on_Howson.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4608" data-file-height="2592" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hazard_taking_on_Howson.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hazard taking on the <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City_F.C." title="Norwich City F.C.">Norwich City</a> defence for <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in October 2012</div></div></div>
<p>Hazard primarily plays as either an <a href="/wiki/Attacking_midfielders" class="mw-redirect" title="Attacking midfielders">attacking midfielder</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Left_winger" class="mw-redirect" title="Left winger">winger</a> and has been credited as being "possibly the outstanding talent in Europe right now".<sup id="cite_ref-303" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-303">&#91;303&#93;</a></sup> At Lille under former manager Rudi Garcia, Hazard often played in the latter role in the team's 433 formation and regularly switched flanks because he could use both feet. Following the departures of fellow <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmakers</a> <a href="/wiki/Yohan_Cabaye" title="Yohan Cabaye">Yohan Cabaye</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gervinho" title="Gervinho">Gervinho</a> in 2011, during the 201112 season, Garcia played Hazard in a creative role as a central attacking midfielder, while also allowing the player to roam back onto the wing if necessary. Two of Hazard's most common exemplary traits are his pace and <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">technical ability</a>, which have been described as "astonishing" and "mesmerizing".<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_fifa_63-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_fifa-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> His speed, acceleration, and dribbling skills, combined with his creativity,<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_espn_304-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_espn-304">&#91;304&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-305" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-305">&#91;305&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-306" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-306">&#91;306&#93;</a></sup> as well as his flair, balance, agility, and low centre of gravity, courtesy of his diminutive stature (1.73 m/5 feet 8 inches),<sup id="cite_ref-307" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-307">&#91;307&#93;</a></sup> allow him to retain possession, take on defenders, and beat opponents in one on one situations.<sup id="cite_ref-308" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-308">&#91;308&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-309" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-309">&#91;309&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At Chelsea, Hazard matured into a world class player and was primarily utilised as a left midfielder, a position which enables him to cut into the centre and strike on goal with his stronger right foot.<sup id="cite_ref-310" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-310">&#91;310&#93;</a></sup> His development into one of the world's best players was highlighted in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Premier_League" title="201415 Premier League">201415 Season</a>; during this season he won multiple awards<sup id="cite_ref-311" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-311">&#91;311&#93;</a></sup> and received praise from pundits and manager alike. Manager Jose Mourinho praised Hazard, saying that "He is already a top player and his evolution has been fantastic. He is still very young and he can become the best player in the world."<sup id="cite_ref-312" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-312">&#91;312&#93;</a></sup> Hazard's former teammate and Lille <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> <a href="/wiki/Rio_Mavuba" title="Rio Mavuba">Rio Mavuba</a> described Hazard as "a great player, with an immense talent. He's actually not that big, but he's so fast. He's also very difficult to dispossess and his finishing is top notch".<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_fifa_63-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_fifa-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Hazard's frequent <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">goal celebration</a> saw him sliding on his knees; since 2018 he has stayed on his feet.<sup id="cite_ref-313" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-313">&#91;313&#93;</a></sup> Although Hazard's favoured role is as a left winger, he is a versatile <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">attacker</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Scheda_giocatore_314-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scheda_giocatore-314">&#91;314&#93;</a></sup> and has also been deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Second_striker" title="Forward (association football)">second striker</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-315" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-315">&#91;315&#93;</a></sup> as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">lone striker</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-316" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-316">&#91;316&#93;</a></sup> or even as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#False_9" title="Forward (association football)">false-9</a> on occasion throughout his career.<sup id="cite_ref-317" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-317">&#91;317&#93;</a></sup> Beyond his speed, creativity, technical skills, and offensive qualities, he is also an accurate <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a><sup id="cite_ref-318" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-318">&#91;318&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">free kick</a> taker.<sup id="cite_ref-Scheda_giocatore_314-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scheda_giocatore-314">&#91;314&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Reception">Reception</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Reception">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_1_Everton_0_(16325064577).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Chelsea_1_Everton_0_%2816325064577%29.jpg/170px-Chelsea_1_Everton_0_%2816325064577%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="170" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Chelsea_1_Everton_0_%2816325064577%29.jpg/255px-Chelsea_1_Everton_0_%2816325064577%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/Chelsea_1_Everton_0_%2816325064577%29.jpg/340px-Chelsea_1_Everton_0_%2816325064577%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2786" data-file-height="2786" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_1_Everton_0_(16325064577).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Acclaimed for his dribbling, creativity and ball retention skills, the <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> website regards Hazard as being "difficult to dispossess."<sup id="cite_ref-319" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-319">&#91;319&#93;</a></sup></div></div></div>
<p>Hazard's pace, coupled with his finishing and ability to retain possession, led to his former coach <a href="/wiki/Claude_Puel" title="Claude Puel">Claude Puel</a> dubbing him "little <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Messi</a>", in reference to the <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> player.<sup id="cite_ref-320" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-320">&#91;320&#93;</a></sup> Puel's sentiments were later echoed by former <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a> manager and <a href="/wiki/Media_personality" class="mw-redirect" title="Media personality">media personality</a> <a href="/wiki/Rolland_Courbis" title="Rolland Courbis">Rolland Courbis</a> who commented "At times it looks to me like Lionel Messi on the right-hand side".<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_fourfourtwo_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_fourfourtwo-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Hazard's "flair and tricky" style of play has been described as being similar to <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> player <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>; a comparison later repeated by former <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">French international</a> <a href="/wiki/Christophe_Dugarry" title="Christophe Dugarry">Christophe Dugarry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-321" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-321">&#91;321&#93;</a></sup> His vision, described as being the trait he has improved on the most, coupled with his passing, has also allowed him to develop into an effective playmaker and assist provider,<sup id="cite_ref-322" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-322">&#91;322&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-323" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-323">&#91;323&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-324" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-324">&#91;324&#93;</a></sup> which in turn, combined with his finishing ability, enables him to both score and create goals.<sup id="cite_ref-Scheda_giocatore_314-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scheda_giocatore-314">&#91;314&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-next_Messi_325-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-next_Messi-325">&#91;325&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In Belgium, Hazard's talent and similar ascension up the country's football hierarchy has led to comparisons to former Belgian international <a href="/wiki/Enzo_Scifo" title="Enzo Scifo">Enzo Scifo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-eden_hazard_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eden_hazard-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-hazard_scifo_326-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_scifo-326">&#91;326&#93;</a></sup> Both players share the same birthplace and Scifo himself spent time with Hazard while he was in Tubize admitting "Eden, you know, I've coached in Tubize. During the week, I took care of the young people at least once, and he, in those days, I immediately saw he had a secure future".<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_scifo_326-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_scifo-326">&#91;326&#93;</a></sup> Former Chelsea player <a href="/wiki/Gianfranco_Zola" title="Gianfranco Zola">Gianfranco Zola</a> likened Hazard to himself in 2019,<sup id="cite_ref-327" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-327">&#91;327&#93;</a></sup> a view which was the Belgian's former club teammate Frank Lampard had previously expressed in 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-Lampard_compare_Hazard_to_Zola_128-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lampard_compare_Hazard_to_Zola-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, despite the positive opinions, Hazard has endured criticism from some. In 2010, former Belgium national team manager Georges Leekens questioned Hazard's work-rate.<sup id="cite_ref-328" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-328">&#91;328&#93;</a></sup> Lille youth academy director Jean-Michel Vandamme countered both managers' criticism by arguing that Hazard simply possesses an intellectual honesty that is out of the ordinary and unexpected of today's footballer declaring "He is a real competitor, not a cheat, nor a moaner, because you don't hear him complaining when he gets fouled".<sup id="cite_ref-hazard_fourfourtwo_62-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hazard_fourfourtwo-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Outside_football">Outside football</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Outside football">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Hazard is married to Natacha Van Honacker. On 19 December 2010, it was reported that she had given birth to a baby boy, Yannis. She gave birth to their second son, Leo, in February 2013,<sup id="cite_ref-329" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-329">&#91;329&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-330" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-330">&#91;330&#93;</a></sup> and a third son, Samy, in September 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-331" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-331">&#91;331&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 November 2020, he tested positive for <a href="/wiki/COVID-19" title="COVID-19">COVID-19</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-332" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-332">&#91;332&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sponsorship">Sponsorship</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Sponsorship">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In 2012, Hazard signed a sponsorship deal with sportswear and equipment supplier, <a href="/wiki/Nike,_Inc." title="Nike, Inc.">Nike</a>. He appeared in an advert for the Nike Green Speed II alongside <a href="/wiki/Mario_G%C3%B6tze" title="Mario Götze">Mario Götze</a>, <a href="/wiki/Theo_Walcott" title="Theo Walcott">Theo Walcott</a>, <a href="/wiki/Raheem_Sterling" title="Raheem Sterling">Raheem Sterling</a>, <a href="/wiki/Christian_Eriksen" title="Christian Eriksen">Christian Eriksen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stephan_El_Shaarawy" title="Stephan El Shaarawy">Stephan El Shaarawy</a> in November 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-333" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-333">&#91;333&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-334" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-334">&#91;334&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hazard features on the cover of <a href="/wiki/EA_Sports" title="EA Sports">EA Sports</a>' <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i></a> video game <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_15" title="FIFA 15">FIFA 15</a></i> in Belgium, the UK, the Netherlands and France, along with <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-335" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-335">&#91;335&#93;</a></sup> Hazard, <a href="/wiki/Marco_Reus" title="Marco Reus">Marco Reus</a>, <a href="/wiki/James_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="James Rodríguez">James Rodríguez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Martial" title="Anthony Martial">Anthony Martial</a> were announced as the official ambassadors of the game and were the finalists to be the new face of <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_17" title="FIFA 17">FIFA 17</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-336" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-336">&#91;336&#93;</a></sup> Hazard was named the new face of the franchise in 2019  taking over from <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>  appearing as the cover star of the regular edition of <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_20" title="FIFA 20">FIFA 20</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-337" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-337">&#91;337&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Since March 2016, Hazard has been appearing in adverts for Belgium-based <a href="/wiki/Lotus_Bakeries" title="Lotus Bakeries">Lotus Bakeries</a> promoting their Biscoff biscuit range. The advert shows him successfully taking a <a href="/wiki/Free_kick" title="Free kick">free kick</a>, sending a ball into a gap in 10,000 cups.<sup id="cite_ref-338" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-338">&#91;338&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_ownership">Club ownership</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Club ownership">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 26 June 2017, Hazard became a part-owner of expansion <a href="/wiki/North_American_Soccer_League" title="North American Soccer League">North American Soccer League</a> franchise <a href="/wiki/San_Diego_1904_FC" title="San Diego 1904 FC">San Diego 1904 FC</a> to begin play in 2018, alongside <a href="/wiki/Demba_Ba" title="Demba Ba">Demba Ba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yohan_Cabaye" title="Yohan Cabaye">Yohan Cabaye</a> and <a href="/wiki/Moussa_Sow" title="Moussa Sow">Moussa Sow</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-339" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-339">&#91;339&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Eden_Hazard&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/1982_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1982 FIFA World Cup">1982</a>:</b> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team"><img alt="Brazil" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/15px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="11" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/23px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/30px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="504" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Paulo_Roberto_Falc%C3%A3o" title="Paulo Roberto Falcão">Falcão</a></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/1986_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1986 FIFA World Cup">1986</a>:</b> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team"><img alt="West Germany" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/15px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="9" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/30px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Toni_Schumacher" title="Toni Schumacher">Schumacher</a></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/1990_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1990 FIFA World Cup">1990</a>:</b> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team"><img alt="West Germany" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/15px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="9" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/30px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Lothar_Matth%C3%A4us" title="Lothar Matthäus">Matthäus</a></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/1994_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1994 FIFA World Cup">1994</a>:</b> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team"><img alt="Italy" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/15px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="10" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/30px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Baggio" title="Roberto Baggio">Baggio</a></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998</a>:</b> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team"><img alt="Croatia" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Flag_of_Croatia.svg/15px-Flag_of_Croatia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="8" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Flag_of_Croatia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Croatia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Flag_of_Croatia.svg/30px-Flag_of_Croatia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Davor_%C5%A0uker" title="Davor uker">uker</a></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/2002_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2002 FIFA World Cup">2002</a>:</b> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team"><img alt="Brazil" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/15px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="11" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/23px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/30px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="504" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006</a>:</b> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team"><img alt="Italy" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/15px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="10" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/30px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Cannavaro" title="Fabio Cannavaro">Cannavaro</a></li>

<li><b><a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014</a>:</b> <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team"><img alt="Germany" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/15px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="9" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/30px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Thomas_M%C3%BCller" title="Thomas Müller">Müller</a></li>

</div></td></tr><tr><td class="navbox-abovebelow" colspan="2" style="background:silver;"><div><b>Silver Ball was first awarded in <a href="/wiki/1982_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1982 FIFA World Cup">1982</a>, and previous winners are uncertain.</b></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>

<ul><li><span class="nowrap">1995: <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/England" title="England"><img alt="England" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/15px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="9" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/30px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="480" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Alan_Shearer" title="Alan Shearer">Shearer</a></span></li>
<li><span class="nowrap">1996: <span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark"><img alt="Denmark" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/15px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="11" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/23px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/30px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="387" /></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Peter_Schmeichel" title="Peter Schmeichel">Schmeichel</a></span></li>
